<Text>The experience of a product is partially based on the product, but substantially based on the service and personal interaction of the product specialists.

My Miracle Ear hearing aides are without a doubt a quality product. They are extremely comfortable (don't even know they are there), and help restore my lost hearing. But what makes these outstanding is the service I receive.

Alan truly cares about me and my hearing. He has spent as much time as I needed and exposed options I didn't even know were available. (ot extra charge options, just options for a better hearing experience) He has never tried to upsell me. After the first series of appointments to fine tune the hearing aides, I have an appointment every 3 months for cleaning, replacing od any needed parts, and a general check up. There is no extra charge for this. It's part of the outstanding customer service.

I recently had my first annual hearing test and Alan made some further refinements and made my hearing even better. Again, no extra charge.

I highly recommend this particular Miracle Ear. I have not been to any others, but I have no need to try any others either.</Text>< pics>

<Rating>5</Rating>< Text>
I highly recommend Miracle-Ear for your hearing aid needs - I give them an "A+".  Alan and Julie are both very kind and make the visit very enjoyable and relaxing.  Alan is exceptional at fine-tuning the hearing aids, providing follow-up care, and answering your questions.  Miracle-Ear explains also about hearing loss and why hearing aids are good for your health beyond just being able to hear well again.  You will also learn that not all hearing aids are equal and the more expensive ones have more frequency switches to fine-tune the hearing aids for your hearing loss.  People don't always lose hearing uniformly across all frequencies so the frequency switches help fine tune them so you can hear across all frequencies again.  Alan was also incredibly patient with my 90-year old dad through the entire process.<//Text>

We came here for brunch on a Saturday. Staff were exceptionally friendly and helpful. Given its location, I imagine this place is busiest on weekdays after work. On Saturday, it had more customers than I expected but still plenty of capacity - so a good place if you fancy brunch but don't want to wait for ages. <Pics>None<//Pics><user_id>109343288040597598057</user_id><review>Dirty" is the correct name for this restaurant because that's how they will treat you.  We went here after seeing Hamilton a few months ago.  They even advertised in the program guide.    We had the early showing so we arrived at the restaurant without reservations around 5:30 pm.  The restaurant was empty except for one other party.

There was 6 of us in our party.  We notified the hostess that we saw the advertisement in the program guide and asked if we could be seated.  She said that they were completely booked but we could sit at a high table in the bar.  Ok, fine.  I guess there would be a mad rush within the next 30-45 minutes that they need to accommodate.  ( We were there about 45 minutes),  By the time we left 90% of the restaurant was still empty

We ordered a variety of appetizers, no alcohol and small plates.  All adequate but nothing to brag about.  The service was average.  It should have been excellent given we were the only table she was serving.  We had to ask for water twice.

Now, the biggest reason why I call them "dirty" is this.  My friend insisted he pay for our meal.  For him this is a big expense.  He paid with his credit card and left  $60 cash for the tip (20%). I asked him to see the receipt given the gratuity amount he was leaving.  There was already an 18% tip included on the bill.

My wife asked the server to return the $60 because our friend was not made aware of this nor did they circle it on the receipt which they typically do. This place is more 4.5 stars. I was so pleasantly surprised; what a neighborhood gem!!  Great service, excellent wine recommendations and the food..... soooooo good.

You will not be disappointed!  We had the warm spinach salad, the burrata bruschetta, the Maccarune Cu Salsiccia (baked rigatoni with Italian sausage) was a delight!  I also had the special that day which was a multi-hour ragu sauce over papperadelle. Yum.<//review>

< Text>
Captain of a class C tall ship embarking on a circumnavigation... Recently anchored in Santa Barbara and our Lofran windlass got stuck in the on position. No damage because I already had 200' of chain down but would have been disastrous had I only had 10' of chain down, could have taken down the masts! Called Danny at Sailing Supply and we determined that old solenoids were the issue. Danny personally drove to the location to pick up the parts and I received them within a day.
